<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h2 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.0688525s;" class="preFade fadeIn">Privacy Policy</h2><p class="sqsrte-small preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.0737705s;">Last Updated: January 4, 2022</p><p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.0786885s;">Thank you for choosing to be part of our community at Outpost4 LLC (“<strong>Company</strong>”<strong>, </strong>“<strong>we</strong>”<strong>, </strong>“<strong>us</strong>”<strong>, </strong>“<strong>our</strong>”). We are committed to protecting your personal information and your right to privacy. If you have any questions or concerns about this privacy notice, or our practices with regards to your personal information, please contact us at hello@outpost4.net. </p><p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.0836066s;">When you visit our website <a href="https://outpost4.net">https://outpost4.net</a> (the "<strong>Website</strong>"),  or use any of our games, software, products, features, or services (the "<strong>Services</strong>"), we appreciate that you are trusting us with your personal information. We take your privacy very seriously. In this privacy notice, we seek to explain to you in the clearest way possible what information we collect, how we use it and what rights you have in relation to it. We hope you take some time to read through it carefully, as it is important. If there are any terms in this privacy notice that you do not agree with, please discontinue use of our Services immediately.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.0885246s;">This privacy notice applies to all information collected through our Services (which, as described above, includes our&nbsp;Website), as well as, any related services, sales, marketing or events.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.0934426s;"><strong>Please read this privacy notice carefully as it will help you understand what we do with the information that we collect. </strong></p>

</div></div><div class="sqs-block horizontalrule-block sqs-block-horizontalrule" data-block-type="47" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1615056069009_11348"><div class="sqs-block-content"><hr></div></div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1615056069009_11833"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h4 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.0983607s;" class="preFade">Personal Information We Collect</h4><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.103279s;">We collect personal information that you voluntarily provide to us when you express an interest in obtaining information about us or our products and Services, when you participate in activities on the&nbsp;or otherwise when you contact us. The personal information we collect may include the following: email addresses and other similar information. </p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.108197s;">All personal information that you provide to us must be true, complete and accurate, and you must notify us of any changes to such personal information.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.113115s;">When interacting with or purchasing Outpost4 Services or products via third party vendors, those parties will have access to your contact information and payment information as voluntarily provided by you. Outpost4 does not store personal identifying or financial information on behalf of our users.</p>
</div>



</div></div><div class="sqs-block horizontalrule-block sqs-block-horizontalrule" data-block-type="47" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1615056069009_16971"><div class="sqs-block-content"><hr></div></div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1615056069009_17587"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h4 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.118033s;" class="preFade">How We Use Personal Information</h4><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.122951s;"><em>In Short: We process your information for purposes based on legitimate business interests, the fulfillment of our contract with you, compliance with our legal obligations, and/or your consent.</em></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.127869s;">We use personal information collected via our Website for a variety of business purposes described below. We process your personal information for these purposes in reliance on our legitimate business interests, in order to enter into or perform a contract with you, with your consent, and/or for compliance with our legal obligations. We indicate the specific processing grounds we rely on next to each purpose listed below. </p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.132787s;">We use the information we collect or receive: </p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.137705s;"><strong>To deliver and facilitate delivery of services to the user.</strong> We may use your information to provide you with the requested service.</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.142623s;"><strong>To respond to user inquiries/offer support to users.</strong> We may use your information to respond to your inquiries and solve any potential issues you might have with the use of our Services.</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.147541s;"><strong>To send you marketing and promotional communications.</strong> We and/or our third-party marketing partners may use the personal information you send to us for our marketing purposes, if this is in accordance with your marketing preferences. For example, when expressing an interest in obtaining information about us or our Website, subscribing to marketing or otherwise contacting us, we will collect personal information from you. You can opt-out of our marketing emails at any time </p><p class="preFade" data-rte-preserve-empty="true" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.152459s;"></p></li></ul>

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h4 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.157377s;" class="preFade">Will Your Information Be Shared?</h4><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.162295s;"><em>In Short: We only share information with your consent, to comply with laws, to provide you with services, to protect your rights, or to fulfill business obligations. This does not include trusted third parties who assist us in operating our website, conducting our business, or servicing you, so long as those parties agree to keep this information confidential. </em></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.167213s;">We may include links to or widgets from other third party products or services on our website. These third party sites have separate and independent privacy policies. We have no responsibility or liability for the content and activities resulting from use of any linked sites, and we encourage you to read the privacy policies on any such third party sites, and proceed only if you are comfortable with such terms.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.172131s;">We may process or share your data that we hold based on the following legal basis:</p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.177049s;"><strong>Consent:</strong> We may process your data if you have given us specific consent to use your personal information for a specific purpose.</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.181967s;"><strong>Legitimate Interests:</strong> We may process your data when it is reasonably necessary to achieve our legitimate business interests.</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.186885s;"><strong>Performance of a Contract:</strong> Where we have entered into a contract with you, we may process your personal information to fulfill the terms of our contract. </p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.191803s;"><strong>Legal Obligations:</strong> We may disclose your information where we are legally required to do so in order to comply with applicable law, governmental requests, a judicial proceeding, court order, or legal process, such as in response to a court order or a subpoena (including in response to public authorities to meet national security or law enforcement requirements).</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.196721s;"><strong>Vital Interests:</strong> We may disclose your information where we believe it is necessary to investigate, prevent, or take action regarding potential violations of our policies, suspected fraud, situations involving potential threats to the safety of any person and illegal activities, or as evidence in litigation in which we are involved.</p></li></ul><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.201639s;">More specifically, we may need to process your data or share your personal information in the following situations:</p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.206557s;"><strong>Business Transfers.</strong> We may share or transfer your information in connection with, or during negotiations of, any merger, sale of company assets, financing, or acquisition of all or a portion of our business to another company.</p></li></ul>
</div>



</div></div><div class="sqs-block horizontalrule-block sqs-block-horizontalrule" data-block-type="47" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1615056069009_28333"><div class="sqs-block-content"><hr></div></div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1615066996505_21345"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h4 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.211475s;" class="preFade">How Long Do We Keep Your Information?</h4><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.216393s;"><em>In Short:&nbsp;We keep your information for as long as necessary to fulfill the purposes outlined in this privacy notice unless otherwise required by law.</em></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.221311s;">We will only keep your personal information for as long as it is necessary for the purposes set out in this privacy notice, unless a longer retention period is required or permitted by law (such as tax, accounting or other legal requirements). No purpose in this notice will require us keeping your personal information for longer than 2 years.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.22623s;">When we have no ongoing legitimate business need to process your personal information, we will either delete or anonymize such information, or, if this is not possible (for example, because your personal information has been stored in backup archives), then we will securely store your personal information and isolate it from any further processing until deletion is possible.</p>
</div>



</div></div><div class="sqs-block horizontalrule-block sqs-block-horizontalrule" data-block-type="47" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1615066996505_25130"><div class="sqs-block-content"><hr></div></div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1615056069009_29127"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h4 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.231148s;" class="preFade">How Do We Keep Your Information Safe?</h4><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.236066s;"><em>In Short:&nbsp;We aim to protect your personal information through a system of organizational and technical security measures.</em></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.240984s;">We have implemented appropriate technical and organizational security measures designed to protect the security of any personal information we process. However, despite our safeguards and efforts to secure your information, no electronic transmission over the Internet or information storage technology can be guaranteed to be 100% secure, so we cannot promise or guarantee that hackers, cybercriminals, or other unauthorized third parties will not be able to defeat our security, and improperly collect, access, steal, or modify your information. Although we will do our best to protect your personal information, transmission of personal information to and from our Website is at your own risk. You should only access the Website within a secure environment.</p>
</div>

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h4 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.245902s;" class="preFade">What Are Your Privacy Rights?</h4><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.25082s;"><em>In Short: You may review, change, or terminate your account at any time.</em></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.255738s;">If you are a resident in the European Economic Area and you believe we are unlawfully processing your personal information, you also have the right to complain to your local data protection supervisory authority. You can find their contact details here: <a href="http://ec.europa.eu/justice/data-protection/bodies/authorities/index_en.htm.">http://ec.europa.eu/justice/data-protection/bodies/authorities/index_en.htm.</a> If you are a resident in Switzerland, the contact details for the data protection authorities are available here: <a href="https://www.edoeb.admin.ch/edoeb/en/home.html.">https://www.edoeb.admin.ch/edoeb/en/home.html.</a> </p>

</div></div><div class="sqs-block horizontalrule-block sqs-block-horizontalrule" data-block-type="47" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1615066996505_35973"><div class="sqs-block-content"><hr></div></div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1615066996505_37049"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h4 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.260656s;" class="preFade">Do California Residents Have Specific Privacy Rights?</h4><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.265574s;"><em>In Short:&nbsp;Yes, if you are a resident of California, you are granted specific rights regarding access to your personal information.</em></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.270492s;">California Civil Code Section 1798.83, also known as the "Shine The Light" law, permits our users who are California residents to request and obtain from us, once a year and free of charge, information about categories of personal information (if any) we disclosed to third parties for direct marketing purposes and the names and addresses of all third parties with which we shared personal information in the immediately preceding calendar year. If you are a California resident and would like to make such a request, please submit your request in writing to us using the contact information provided below.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.27541s;">If you are under 18 years of age, reside in California, and have a registered account with the Website, you have the right to request removal of unwanted data that you publicly post on the Website. To request removal of such data, please contact us using the contact information provided below, and include the email address associated with your account and a statement that you reside in California. We will make sure the data is not publicly displayed on the Website, but please be aware that the data may not be completely or comprehensively removed from all our systems (e.g. backups, etc.).</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.280328s;"><strong>CCPA Privacy Notice</strong></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.285246s;">The California Code of Regulations defines a "<strong>resident</strong>" as:</p><ol data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.290164s;">Every individual who is in the State of California for other than a temporary or transitory purpose and </p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.295082s;">Every individual who is domiciled in the State of California who is outside the State of California for a temporary or transitory purpose</p></li></ol><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.3s;">All other individuals are defined as "<strong>non-residents</strong>."</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.304918s;">If this definition of "<strong>resident</strong>" applies to you, we must adhere to certain rights and obligations regarding your personal information.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.309836s;">What categories of personal information do we collect?</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.314754s;">We have collected the following categories of personal information in the past twelve (12) months:</p>
</div>

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.319672s;">We may also collect other personal information outside of these categories instances where you interact with us in-person, online, or by phone or mail in the context of:</p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.32459s;">Receiving help through our customer support channels;</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.329508s;">Participation in customer surveys or contests; and</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.334426s;">Facilitation in the delivery of our Services and to respond to your inquiries.</p></li></ul><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.339344s;"><strong>How do we use and share your personal information?</strong></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.344262s;">More information about our data collection and sharing practices can be found in this privacy notice. You may contact us by email at hello@outpost4.net.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.34918s;">If you are using an authorized agent to exercise your right to opt-out we may deny a request if the authorized agent does not submit proof that they have been validly authorized to act on your behalf.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.354098s;"><strong>Will your information be shared with anyone else?</strong></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.359016s;">We may disclose your personal information with our service providers pursuant to a written contract between us and each service provider. Each service provider is a for-profit entity that processes the information on our behalf.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.363934s;">We may use your personal information for our own business purposes, such as for undertaking internal research for technological development and demonstration. This is not considered to be "selling" of your personal data. </p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.368852s;">Outpost4 LLC&nbsp;has not disclosed or sold any personal information to third parties for a business or commercial purpose in the preceding 12 months. Outpost4 LLC will not sell personal information in the future belonging to website visitors, users and other consumers.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.37377s;"><strong>Your rights with respect to your personal data</strong></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.378689s;"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Right to request deletion of the data - Request to delete</span></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.383607s;">You can ask for the deletion of your personal information. If you ask us to delete your personal information, we will respect your request and delete your personal information, subject to certain exceptions provided by law, such as (but not limited to) the exercise by another consumer of his or her right to free speech, our compliance requirements resulting from a legal obligation or any processing that may be required to protect against illegal activities.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.388525s;"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Right to be informed - Request to know</span></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.393443s;">Depending on the circumstances, you have a right to know:</p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.398361s;">whether we collect and use your personal information;</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.403279s;">the categories of personal information that we collect;</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.408197s;">the purposes for which the collected personal information is used;</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.413115s;">whether we sell your personal information to third parties;</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.418033s;">the categories of personal information that we sold or disclosed for a business purpose;</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.422951s;">the categories of third parties to whom the personal information was sold or disclosed for a business purpose; and</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.427869s;">the business or commercial purpose for collecting or selling personal information.</p></li></ul><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.432787s;">In accordance with applicable law, we are not obligated to provide or delete consumer information that is de-identified in response to a consumer request or to re-identify individual data to verify a consumer request.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.437705s;"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Right to Non-Discrimination for the Exercise of a Consumer’s Privacy Rights</span></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.442623s;">We will not discriminate against you if you exercise your privacy rights.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.447541s;"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Verification process</span></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.452459s;">Upon receiving your request, we will need to verify your identity to determine you are the same person about whom we have the information in our system. These verification efforts require us to ask you to provide information so that we can match it with information you have previously provided us. For instance, depending on the type of request you submit, we may ask you to provide certain information so that we can match the information you provide with the information we already have on file, or we may contact you through a communication method (e.g. phone or email) that you have previously provided to us. We may also use other verification methods as the circumstances dictate.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.457377s;">We will only use personal information provided in your request to verify your identity or authority to make the request. To the extent possible, we will avoid requesting additional information from you for the purposes of verification. If, however, we cannot verify your identity from the information already maintained by us, we may request that you provide additional information for the purposes of verifying your identity, and for security or fraud-prevention purposes. We will delete such additionally provided information as soon as we finish verifying you.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.462295s;"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Other privacy rights</span></p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.467213s;">you may object to the processing of your personal data</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.472131s;">you may request correction of your personal data if it is incorrect or no longer relevant, or ask to restrict the processing of the data</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.477049s;">you can designate an authorized agent to make a request under the CCPA on your behalf. We may deny a request from an authorized agent that does not submit proof that they have been validly authorized to act on your behalf in accordance with the CCPA.</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.481967s;">you may request to opt-out from future selling of your personal information to third parties. Upon receiving a request to opt-out, we will act upon the request as soon as feasibly possible, but no later than 15 days from the date of the request submission.</p></li></ul><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.486885s;">To exercise these rights, you can contact us&nbsp;by email at hello@outpost4.net or by referring to the contact details at the bottom of this document. If you have a complaint about how we handle your data, we would like to hear from you.</p>
</div>

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h4 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.491803s;" class="preFade">Parental Guidelines</h4><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.496721s;">We will not collect any personally identifiable information from children thirteen (13) years of age or younger without prior verifiable parental consent. When verifiable parental consent is not obtained, we may only use the online contact information (such as email) to:</p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.501639s;">(i) respond directly to the child's request on a one-time basis and not use that information to re-contact the child for other purposes. Once we have responded to such request we will delete the information provided immediately;</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.506557s;">(ii) request the name or online contact information of a parent for the purpose of obtaining verifiable parental consent or providing parental notification; and</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.511475s;">(iii) respond more than once directly to a specific request from a child and not used to re-contact the child for other purposes. We will use our best efforts to provide parental notification, which will include the nature and intended use as well as an opportunity for the parent to prevent the use of the information and participation in the activity.</p></li></ul><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.516393s;">We will never condition a child’s use of our site on the child disclosing more personal information than is reasonably necessary to use our website.</p>
